# Task: Map Test Coverage Gaps in Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

**Repository:** apache/kafka
**Output:** Write your analysis to `/workspace/coverage_analysis.md`

## Objective

Identify test coverage gaps in Kafka's consumer group coordinator. The group coordinator manages consumer group membership, partition assignment, and offset commits for Kafka consumers.

## Scope

Focus on:
- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.scala` — main coordinator logic
- `core/src/test/scala/unit/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorTest.scala` — existing tests
- `core/src/main/scala/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadata.scala` — group state machine

## Content Expectations

Your analysis must:
1. **Identify at least 5 specific failure modes** that are not tested in `GroupCoordinatorTest.scala`
2. **Propose a regression test** for each failure mode (class name, test method signature, key assertions)
3. **Estimate the coverage delta** each proposed test would add (which code paths would it hit)
4. **Label risk level**: HIGH / MEDIUM / LOW

## Output Format

Write to `/workspace/coverage_analysis.md`:

```markdown
# Test Coverage Gap Analysis: Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

## Summary

## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests

### Failure Mode 1: [Name]
- **Risk**: HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW
- **Code Location**: GroupCoordinator.scala ~line NNN
- **Description**: [What failure scenario is untested]
- **Proposed Test**:
  ```java
  @Test
  public void testXxx() { ... }
  ```
- **Coverage Delta**: [Which code paths this test would exercise]

[Repeat for 5+ failure modes]

## File References
```

## Anti-Requirements
- Do not fabricate class or method names — read the actual source first
- Each gap must reference a specific file and approximate location
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

  6210→    public CoordinatorResult<Void, CoordinatorRecord> classicGroupJoin(
  6211→        AuthorizableRequestContext context,
  6212→        JoinGroupRequestData request,
  6213→        CompletableFuture<JoinGroupResponseData> responseFuture
  6214→    ) {
  6215→        Group group = groups.get(request.groupId(), Long.MAX_VALUE);
  6216→        if (group != null) {
  6217→            if (group.type() == CONSUMER && !group.isEmpty()) {
  6218→                // classicGroupJoinToConsumerGroup takes the join requests to non-empty consumer groups.
  6219→                // The empty consumer groups should be converted to classic groups in classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup.
  6220→                return classicGroupJoinToConsumerGroup((ConsumerGroup) group, context, request, responseFuture);
  6221→            } else if (group.type() == CONSUMER || group.type() == CLASSIC || group.type() == STREAMS && group.isEmpty()) {
  6222→                // classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup accepts:
  6223→                // - classic groups
  6224→                // - empty streams groups
  6225→                // - empty consumer groups
  6226→                return classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup(context, request, responseFuture);
  6227→            } else {
  6228→                // Group exists but it's not a consumer group
  6229→                responseFuture.complete(new JoinGroupResponseData()
  6230→                    .setMemberId(UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID)
  6231→                    .setErrorCode(Errors.INCONSISTENT_GROUP_PROTOCOL.code())
  6232→                );
  6233→                return EMPTY_RESULT;
  6234→            }
  6235→        } else {
  6236→            return classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup(context, request, responseFuture);
  6237→        }
  6238→    }

54-usertool_resultRead
  6810→    private CoordinatorResult<Void, CoordinatorRecord> expireClassicGroupMemberHeartbeat(
  6811→        String groupId,
  6812→        String memberId
  6813→    ) {
  6814→        ClassicGroup group;
  6815→        try {
  6816→            group = getOrMaybeCreateClassicGroup(groupId, false);
  6817→        } catch (GroupIdNotFoundException exception) {
  6818→            log.debug("Received notification of heartbeat expiration for member {} after group {} " +
  6819→                "had already been deleted or upgraded.", memberId, groupId);
  6820→            return EMPTY_RESULT;
  6821→        }
  6822→
  6823→        if (group.isInState(DEAD)) {
  6824→            log.info("Received notification of heartbeat expiration for member {} after group {} " +
  6825→                    "had already been unloaded or deleted.",
  6826→                memberId, group.groupId());
  6827→        } else if (group.isPendingMember(memberId)) {
  6828→            log.info("Pending member {} in group {} has been removed after session timeout expiration.",
  6829→                memberId, group.groupId());

  1504→    private void throwIfConsumerGroupIsFull(
  1505→        ConsumerGroup group,
  1506→        String memberId
  1507→    ) throws GroupMaxSizeReachedException {
  1508→        // If the consumer group has reached its maximum capacity, the member is rejected if it is not
  1509→        // already a member of the consumer group.
  1510→        if (group.numMembers() >= config.consumerGroupMaxSize() && (memberId.isEmpty() || !group.hasMember(memberId))) {
  1511→            throw new GroupMaxSizeReachedException("The consumer group has reached its maximum capacity of "
  1512→                + config.consumerGroupMaxSize() + " members.");
  1513→        }
  1514→    }
  1515→

  1525→    private void throwIfShareGroupIsFull(

  1530→        // a member of the share group.

  1532→            throw new GroupMaxSizeReachedException("The share group has reached its maximum capacity of "
  1533→                + config.shareGroupMaxSize() + " members.");

## Summary of Findings

Five concrete, untested failure modes were identified by reading the actual source code and cross-referencing every test method in the existing test suite:

| # | Failure Mode | Risk | File / Line |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | **`classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup` append failure** — `appendFuture.whenComplete` has no error handler, so `responseFuture` hangs forever when a log write fails | HIGH | `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~7601 |
| 2 | **`expirePendingSync` with stale generation** — mismatch between timer's `generationId` and current group generation is only logged; no cleanup of current-generation pending sync members | MEDIUM | `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~7253 |
| 3 | **Follower leave during `COMPLETING_REBALANCE`** — `removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup` completes the join future but never completes `awaitingSyncFuture`, leaving the member's SyncGroup response stuck | MEDIUM | `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~8098, `ClassicGroup.java` ~478 |
| 4 | **Static member temporary leave with pending revocations** — `consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave` unconditionally sets `partitionsPendingRevocation(Map.of())`, silently discarding partitions the member had not yet revoked | MEDIUM | `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~4137 |
| 5 | **`onTopicsDeleted` with pending transactional offsets** — the `pendingTransactionalOffsets.forEach` branch at line 1108–1109 is exercised by no existing test; topic deletion tombstones for in-flight transactions are not validated | MEDIUM | `OffsetMetadataManager.java` ~1108 |

IllegalStateException(\"Attempt to add pending sync member \" + memberId +\n                \" which is already a stable member of the group.\");\n        }\n\n        return pendingSyncMembers.add(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Remove a member that has not yet synced.\n     *\n     * @param memberId the member id.\n     * @return true if the group did store this member, false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean removePendingSyncMember(String memberId) {\n        if (!hasMember(memberId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempt to add pending member \" + memberId +\n                \" which is already a stable member of the group.\");\n        }\n        return pendingSyncMembers.remove(memberId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return true if all members have sent sync group requests,\n     *         false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean hasReceivedSyncFromAllMembers() {\n        return pendingSyncMembers.isEmpty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return members that have yet to sync.\n     */\n    public Set<String> allPendingSyncMembers() {\n        return pendingSyncMembers;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Clear members pending sync.\n     */\n    public void clearPendingSyncMembers() {\n        pendingSyncMembers.clear();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether the given group instance id exists as\n     * a static member.\n     *\n     * @param groupInstanceId the group instance id.\n     * @return true if a static member with the group instance id exists,\n     *         false otherwise.\n     */\n    public boolean hasStaticMember(String groupInstanceId) {\n        return staticMembers.containsKey(groupInstanceId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get member id of a static member that matches the given group\n     * instance id.\n     *\n     * @param groupInstanceId the group instance id.\n     * @return the static member if it exists.\n     */\n    public String staticMemberId(String groupInstanceId) {\n        return staticMembers.get(groupInstanceId);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return members who have yet to rejoin during the\n     *         join group phase.\n     */\n    public Map<String, ClassicGroupMember> notYetRejoinedMembers() {\n        Map<String, ClassicGroupMember> notYetRejoinedMembers = new HashMap<>();\n        members.values().forEach(member -> {\n            if (!member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n                notYetRejoinedMembers.put(member.memberId(), member);\n            }\n        });\n        return notYetRejoinedMembers;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return whether all members have joined.\n     */\n    public boolean hasAllMembersJoined() {\n        return members.size() == numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse && pendingJoinMembers.isEmpty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the ids of all members in the group.\n     */\n    public Set<String> allMemberIds() {\n        return members.keySet();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the ids of all static members in the group.\n     */\n    public Set<String> allStaticMemberIds() {\n        return new HashSet<>(staticMembers.values());\n    }\n\n    // For testing only.\n    public Set<String> allDynamicMemberIds() {\n        Set<String> dynamicMemberSet = new HashSet<>(allMemberIds());\n        staticMembers.values().forEach(dynamicMemberSet::remove);\n        return dynamicMemberSet;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return number of members waiting for a join group response.\n     */\n    public int numAwaitingJoinResponse() {\n        return numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return all members.\n     */\n    public Collection<ClassicGroupMember> allMembers() {\n        return members.values();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the group's rebalance timeout in milliseconds.\n     *         It is the max of all members' rebalance timeout.\n     */\n    public int rebalanceTimeoutMs() {\n        int maxRebalanceTimeoutMs = 0;\n        for (ClassicGroupMember member : members.values()) {\n            maxRebalanceTimeoutMs = Math.max(maxRebalanceTimeoutMs, member.rebalanceTimeoutMs());\n        }\n        return maxRebalanceTimeoutMs;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Generate a member id from the given client and group instance ids.\n     *\n     * @param clientId         the client id.\n     * @param groupInstanceId  the group instance id.\n     * @return the generated id.\n     */\n    public String generateMemberId(String clientId, Optional<String> groupInstanceId) {\n        return groupInstanceId.map(s -> s + MEMBER_ID_DELIMITER + UUID.randomUUID())\n            .orElseGet(() -> clientId + MEMBER_ID_DELIMITER + UUID.randomUUID());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates that (1) the group instance id exists and is mapped to the member id\n     * if the group instance id is provided; and (2) the member id exists in the group.\n     *\n     * @param memberId          The member id.\n     * @param groupInstanceId   The group instance id.\n     * @param operation         The operation.\n     *\n     * @throws UnknownMemberIdException\n     * @throws FencedInstanceIdException\n     */\n    public void validateMember(\n        String memberId,\n        String groupInstanceId,\n        String operation\n    ) throws UnknownMemberIdException, FencedInstanceIdException {\n        if (groupInstanceId != null) {\n            String existingMemberId = staticMemberId(groupInstanceId);\n            if (existingMemberId == null) {\n                throw Errors.UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID.exception();\n            } else if (!existingMemberId.equals(memberId)) {\n                log.info(\"Request memberId={} for static member with groupInstanceId={} \" +\n                         \"is fenced by existing memberId={} during operation {}\",\n                    memberId, groupInstanceId, existingMemberId, operation);\n                throw Errors.FENCED_INSTANCE_ID.exception();\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (!hasMember(memberId)) {\n            throw Errors.UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID.exception();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the OffsetCommit request.\n     *\n     * @param memberId          The member id.\n     * @param groupInstanceId   The group instance id.\n     * @param generationId      The generation id.\n     * @param isTransactional   Whether the offset commit is transactional or not.\n     * @param apiVersion        The api version.\n     * @return A validator for per-partition validation.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public CommitPartitionValidator validateOffsetCommit(\n        String memberId,\n        String groupInstanceId,\n        int generationId,\n        boolean isTransactional,\n        int apiVersion\n    ) throws CoordinatorNotAvailableException, UnknownMemberIdException, IllegalGenerationException, FencedInstanceIdException {\n        if (isInState(DEAD)) {\n            throw Errors.COORDINATOR_NOT_AVAILABLE.exception();\n        }\n\n        if (generationId < 0 && isInState(EMPTY)) {\n            // When the generation id is -1, the request comes from either the admin client\n            // or a consumer which does not use the group management facility. In this case,\n            // the request can commit offsets if the group is empty.\n            return CommitPartitionValidator.NO_OP;\n        }\n\n        if (generationId >= 0 || !memberId.isEmpty() || groupInstanceId != null) {\n            validateMember(memberId, groupInstanceId, isTransactional ? \"offset-commit\" : \"txn-offset-commit\");\n\n            if (generationId != this.generationId) {\n                throw Errors.ILLEGAL_GENERATION.exception();\n            }\n        } else if (!isTransactional && !isInState(EMPTY)) {\n            // If the request does not contain the member id and the generation id (version 0),\n            // offset commits are only accepted when the group is empty.\n            // This does not apply to transactional offset commits, since the older versions\n            // of this protocol do not require member id and generation id.\n            throw Errors.UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID.exception();\n        }\n\n        if (!isTransactional && isInState(COMPLETING_REBALANCE)) {\n            // We should not receive a commit request if the group has not completed rebalance;\n            // but since the consumer's member.id and generation is valid, it means it has received\n            // the latest group generation information from the JoinResponse.\n            // So let's return a REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS to let consumer handle it gracefully.\n            // This does not apply to transactional offset commits, since the group state\n            // is not enforced for those.\n            throw Errors.REBALANCE_IN_PROGRESS.exception();\n        }\n\n        return CommitPartitionValidator.NO_OP;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the OffsetFetch request.\n     *\n     * @param memberId              The member id. This is not provided for classic groups.\n     * @param memberEpoch           The member epoch for consumer groups. This is not provided for classic groups.\n     * @param lastCommittedOffset   The last committed offsets in the timeline.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void validateOffsetFetch(\n        String memberId,\n        int memberEpoch,\n        long lastCommittedOffset\n    ) throws GroupIdNotFoundException {\n        if (isInState(DEAD)) {\n            throw new GroupIdNotFoundException(String.format(\"Group %s is in dead state.\", groupId));\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the OffsetDelete request.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void validateOffsetDelete() throws ApiException {\n        switch (currentState()) {\n            case DEAD:\n                throw new GroupIdNotFoundException(String.format(\"Group %s is in dead state.\", groupId));\n            case STABLE:\n            case PREPARING_REBALANCE:\n            case COMPLETING_REBALANCE:\n                if (!usesConsumerGroupProtocol()) {\n                    throw Errors.NON_EMPTY_GROUP.exception();\n                }\n                break;\n            default:\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the DeleteGroups request.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void validateDeleteGroup() throws ApiException {\n        switch (currentState()) {\n            case DEAD:\n                throw new GroupIdNotFoundException(String.format(\"Group %s is in dead state.\", groupId));\n            case STABLE:\n            case PREPARING_REBALANCE:\n            case COMPLETING_REBALANCE:\n                throw Errors.NON_EMPTY_GROUP.exception();\n            default:\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Populates the list of records with tombstone(s) for deleting the group.\n     *\n     * @param records The list of records.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public void createGroupTombstoneRecords(List<CoordinatorRecord> records) {\n        records.add(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newGroupMetadataTombstoneRecord(groupId()));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isEmpty() {\n        return isInState(EMPTY);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Return the offset expiration condition to be used for this group. This is based on several factors\n     * such as the group state, the protocol type, and the GroupMetadata record version.\n     *\n     * See {@link org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.OffsetExpirationCondition}\n     *\n     * @return The offset expiration condition for the group or Empty if no such condition exists.\n     */\n    @Override\n    public Optional<OffsetExpirationCondition> offsetExpirationCondition() {\n        if (protocolType.isPresent()) {\n            if (isInState(EMPTY)) {\n                // No members exist in the group =>\n                // - If current state timestamp exists and retention period has passed since group became Empty,\n                //   expire all offsets with no pending offset commit;\n                // - If there is no current state timestamp (old group metadata schema) and retention period has passed\n                //   since the last commit timestamp, expire the offset\n                return Optional.of(new OffsetExpirationConditionImpl(\n                    offsetAndMetadata -> currentStateTimestamp.orElse(offsetAndMetadata.commitTimestampMs))\n                );\n            } else if (usesConsumerGroupProtocol() && subscribedTopics.isPresent() && isInState(STABLE)) {\n                // Consumers exist in the group and group is Stable =>\n                // - If the group is aware of the subscribed topics and retention period has passed since the\n                //   last commit timestamp, expire the offset.\n                return Optional.of(new OffsetExpirationConditionImpl(offsetAndMetadata -> offsetAndMetadata.commitTimestampMs));\n            }\n        } else {\n            // protocolType is None => standalone (simple) consumer, that uses Kafka for offset storage. Only\n            // expire offsets where retention period has passed since their last commit.\n            return Optional.of(new OffsetExpirationConditionImpl(offsetAndMetadata -> offsetAndMetadata.commitTimestampMs));\n        }\n        // If none of the conditions above are met, do not expire any offsets.\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isInStates(Set<String> statesFilter, long committedOffset) {\n        return statesFilter.contains(state.toLowerCaseString());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return whether the group can rebalance.\n     */\n    public boolean canRebalance() {\n        return PREPARING_REBALANCE.validPreviousStates().contains(state);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Transition to a group state.\n     * @param groupState the group state.\n     */\n    public void transitionTo(ClassicGroupState groupState) {\n        assertValidTransition(groupState);\n        previousState = state;\n        state = groupState;\n        currentStateTimestamp = Optional.of(time.milliseconds());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Select a protocol that will be used for this group. Each member\n     * will vote for a protocol and the one with the most votes will\n     * be selected. Only a protocol that is supported by all members\n     * can be selected.\n     *\n     * @return the name of the selected protocol.\n     */\n    public String selectProtocol() {\n        if (members.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Cannot select protocol for empty group\");\n        }\n\n        // select the protocol for this group which is supported by all members\n        Set<String> candidates = candidateProtocols();\n\n        // let each member vote for one of the protocols\n        Map<String, Integer> votesByProtocol = new HashMap<>();\n        allMembers().stream().map(member -> member.vote(candidates))\n            .forEach(protocolName -> {\n                int count = votesByProtocol.getOrDefault(protocolName, 0);\n                votesByProtocol.put(protocolName, count + 1);\n            });\n\n        // choose the one with the most votes\n        return votesByProtocol.entrySet().stream()\n            .max(Comparator.comparingInt(Map.Entry::getValue))\n            .map(Map.Entry::getKey).orElse(null);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Increment the protocol count for all of the member's\n     * supported protocols.\n     *\n     * @param member the member.\n     */\n    private void incrementSupportedProtocols(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        member.supportedProtocols().forEach(protocol -> {\n            int count = supportedProtocols.getOrDefault(protocol.name(), 0);\n            supportedProtocols.put(protocol.name(), count + 1);\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decrement the protocol count for all of the member's\n     * supported protocols.\n     *\n     * @param member the member.\n     */\n    private void decrementSupportedProtocols(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        member.supportedProtocols().forEach(protocol -> {\n            int count = supportedProtocols.getOrDefault(protocol.name(), 0);\n            supportedProtocols.put(protocol.name(), count - 1);\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * A candidate protocol must be supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @return a set of candidate protocols that can be chosen as the protocol\n     *         for the group.\n     */\n    private Set<String> candidateProtocols() {\n        // get the set of protocols that are commonly supported by all members\n        return supportedProtocols.entrySet().stream()\n            .filter(protocol -> protocol.getValue() == members.size())\n            .map(Map.Entry::getKey).collect(Collectors.toSet());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether at least one of the given protocols can be supported. A\n     * protocol can be supported if it is supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @param member               the member to check.\n     *\n     * @return a boolean based on the condition mentioned above.\n     */\n    public boolean supportsProtocols(ClassicGroupMember member) {\n        return supportsProtocols(\n            member.protocolType(),\n            ClassicGroupMember.plainProtocolSet(member.supportedProtocols())\n        );\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether at least one of the given protocols can be supported. A\n     * protocol can be supported if it is supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @param memberProtocolType  the member protocol type.\n     * @param memberProtocols     the set of protocol names.\n     *\n     * @return a boolean based on the condition mentioned above.\n     */\n    public boolean supportsProtocols(\n        String memberProtocolType,\n        JoinGroupRequestProtocolCollection memberProtocols\n    ) {\n        return supportsProtocols(\n            memberProtocolType,\n            ClassicGroupMember.plainProtocolSet(memberProtocols)\n        );\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether at least one of the given protocols can be supported. A\n     * protocol can be supported if it is supported by all members.\n     *\n     * @param memberProtocolType  the member protocol type.\n     * @param memberProtocols     the set of protocol names.\n     *\n     * @return a boolean based on the condition mentioned above.\n     */\n    public boolean supportsProtocols(String memberProtocolType, Set<String> memberProtocols) {\n        if (isInState(EMPTY)) {\n            return !memberProtocolType.isEmpty() && !memberProtocols.isEmpty();\n        } else {\n            return protocolType.map(type -> type.equals(memberProtocolType)).orElse(false) &&\n                memberProtocols.stream()\n                    .anyMatch(name -> supportedProtocols.getOrDefault(name, 0) == members.size());\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the topics that the group is subscribed to.\n     */\n    public Optional<Set<String>> subscribedTopics() {\n        return subscribedTopics;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns true if the classic group is actively subscribed to the topic. When the classic group does not know,\n     * because the information is not available yet or because it has failed to parse the Consumer Protocol, we\n     * consider the group not subscribed to the topic if the group is not using any protocol or not using the\n     * consumer group protocol.\n     *\n     * @param topic  The topic name.\n     *\n     * @return whether the group is subscribed to the topic.\n     */\n    public boolean isSubscribedToTopic(String topic) {\n        return subscribedTopics.map(topics -> topics.contains(topic))\n            .orElse(usesConsumerGroupProtocol());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Collects the set of topics that the members are subscribed to when the Protocol Type is equal\n     * to 'consumer'. Empty is returned if\n     * - the protocol type is not equal to 'consumer';\n     * - the protocol is not defined yet; or\n     * - the protocol metadata does not comply with the schema.\n     *\n     * @return the subscribed topics or Empty based on the condition above.\n     */\n    public Optional<Set<String>> computeSubscribedTopics() {\n        if (protocolType.isEmpty()) {\n            return Optional.empty();\n        }\n        String type = protocolType.get();\n        if (!type.equals(ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE)) {\n            return Optional.empty();\n        }\n        if (members.isEmpty()) {\n            return Optional.of(Set.of());\n        }\n\n        if (protocolName.isPresent()) {\n            try {\n                Set<String> allSubscribedTopics = new HashSet<>();\n                members.values().forEach(member -> {\n                    // The consumer protocol is parsed with V0 which is the based prefix of all versions.\n                    // This way the consumer group manager does not depend on any specific existing or\n                    // future versions of the consumer protocol. VO must prefix all new versions.\n                    ByteBuffer buffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(member.metadata(protocolName.get()));\n                    ConsumerProtocol.deserializeVersion(buffer);\n                    allSubscribedTopics.addAll(new HashSet<>(\n                        ConsumerProtocol.deserializeConsumerProtocolSubscription(buffer, (short) 0).topics()\n                    ));\n                });\n                return Optional.of(allSubscribedTopics);\n            } catch (SchemaException e) {\n                log.warn(\"Failed to parse Consumer Protocol {}:{} of group {}. Consumer group coordinator is not aware of the subscribed topics.\",\n                        ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE, protocolName.get(), groupId, e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Update a member.\n     *\n     * @param member              the member.\n     * @param protocols           the list of protocols.\n     * @param rebalanceTimeoutMs  the rebalance timeout in milliseconds.\n     * @param sessionTimeoutMs    the session timeout in milliseconds.\n     * @param future              the future that is invoked once the join phase is complete.\n     */\n    public void updateMember(\n        ClassicGroupMember member,\n        JoinGroupRequestProtocolCollection protocols,\n        int rebalanceTimeoutMs,\n        int sessionTimeoutMs,\n        CompletableFuture<JoinGroupResponseData> future\n    ) {\n        decrementSupportedProtocols(member);\n        member.setSupportedProtocols(protocols);\n        incrementSupportedProtocols(member);\n        member.setRebalanceTimeoutMs(rebalanceTimeoutMs);\n        member.setSessionTimeoutMs(sessionTimeoutMs);\n\n        if (future != null && !member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse++;\n        } else if (future == null && member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse--;\n        }\n        member.setAwaitingJoinFuture(future);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete the join future.\n     *\n     * @param member    the member.\n     * @param response  the join response to complete the future with.\n     * @return true if a join future actually completes.\n     */\n    public boolean completeJoinFuture(\n        ClassicGroupMember member,\n        JoinGroupResponseData response\n    ) {\n        if (member.isAwaitingJoin()) {\n            member.awaitingJoinFuture().complete(response);\n            member.setAwaitingJoinFuture(null);\n            numMembersAwaitingJoinResponse--;\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete all the awaiting join future with the given error.\n     *\n     * @param error  the error to complete the future with.\n     */\n    public void completeAllJoinFutures(\n        Errors error\n    ) {\n        members.forEach((memberId, member) -> completeJoinFuture(\n            member,\n            new JoinGroupResponseData()\n                .setMemberId(memberId)\n                .setErrorCode(error.code())\n        ));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete a member's sync future.\n     *\n     * @param member    the member.\n     * @param response  the sync response to complete the future with.\n     * @return true if a sync future actually completes.\n     */\n    public boolean completeSyncFuture(\n        ClassicGroupMember member,\n        SyncGroupResponseData response\n    ) {\n        if (member.isAwaitingSync()) {\n            member.awaitingSyncFuture().complete(response);\n            member.setAwaitingSyncFuture(null);\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Complete all the awaiting sync future with the give error.\n     *\n     * @param error  the error to complete the future with.\n     */\n    public void completeAllSyncFutures(\n        Errors error\n    ) {\n        members.forEach((__, member) -> completeSyncFuture(\n            member,\n            new SyncGroupResponseData()\n                .setErrorCode(error.code())\n        ));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Initiate the next generation for the group.\n     */\n    public void initNextGeneration() {\n        generationId++;\n        if (!members.isEmpty()) {\n            setProtocolName(Optional.of(selectProtocol()));\n            subscribedTopics = computeSubscribedTopics();\n            transitionTo(COMPLETING_REBALANCE);\n        } else {\n            setProtocolName(Optional.empty());\n            subscribedTopics = computeSubscribedTopics();\n            transitionTo(EMPTY);\n        }\n        clearPendingSyncMembers();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get all members formatted as a join response.\n     *\n     * @return the members.\n     */\n    public List<JoinGroupResponseMember> currentClassicGroupMembers() {\n        if (isInState(DEAD) || isInState(PREPARING_REBALANCE)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Cannot obtain classic member metadata for group \" +\n                groupId + \" in state \" + state);\n        }\n\n        return members.values().stream().map(member ->\n            new JoinGroupResponseMember()\n                .setMemberId(member.memberId())\n                .setGroupInstanceId(member.groupInstanceId().orElse(null))\n                .setMetadata(member.metadata(protocolName.orElse(null))))\n            .toList();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return the group formatted as a list group response based on the committed offset.\n     */\n    public ListGroupsResponseData.ListedGroup asListedGroup(long committedOffset) {\n        return new ListGroupsResponseData.ListedGroup()\n            .setGroupId(groupId)\n            .setProtocolType(protocolType.orElse(\"\"))\n            .setGroupState(state.toString())\n            .setGroupType(type().toString());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return All member assignments keyed by member id.\n     */\n    public Map<String, byte[]> groupAssignment() {\n        return allMembers().stream().collect(Collectors.toMap(\n            ClassicGroupMember::memberId, ClassicGroupMember::assignment\n        ));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Convert the given ConsumerGroup to a corresponding ClassicGroup.\n     *\n     * @param consumerGroup  The converted ConsumerGroup.\n     * @param leavingMembers The members that will not be converted in the ClassicGroup.\n     * @param joiningMember  The member that needs to be converted and added to the ClassicGroup.\n     *                       When not null, must have an instanceId that matches an existing member.\n     * @param logContext     The logContext to create the ClassicGroup.\n     * @param time           The time to create the ClassicGroup.\n     * @param image          The MetadataImage.\n     * @return The created ClassicGroup.\n     */\n    public static ClassicGroup fromConsumerGroup(\n        ConsumerGroup consumerGroup,\n        Set<ConsumerGroupMember> leavingMembers,\n        ConsumerGroupMember joiningMember,\n        LogContext logContext,\n        Time time,\n        CoordinatorMetadataImage image\n    ) {\n        ClassicGroup classicGroup = new ClassicGroup(\n            logContext,\n            consumerGroup.groupId(),\n            ClassicGroupState.STABLE,\n            time,\n            consumerGroup.groupEpoch(),\n            Optional.of(ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE),\n            Optional.empty(),\n            Optional.empty(),\n            Optional.of(time.milliseconds())\n        );\n\n        consumerGroup.members().forEach((memberId, member) -> {\n            if (!leavingMembers.contains(member) &&\n                (joiningMember == null || joiningMember.instanceId() == null || !joiningMember.instanceId().equals(member.instanceId()))) {\n                classicGroup.add(\n                    new ClassicGroupMember(\n                        memberId,\n                        Optional.ofNullable(member.instanceId()),\n                        member.clientId(),\n                        member.clientHost(),\n                        member.rebalanceTimeoutMs(),\n                        member.classicProtocolSessionTimeout().get(),\n                        ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE,\n                        member.supportedJoinGroupRequestProtocols(),\n                        null\n                    )\n                );\n            }\n        });\n\n        if (joiningMember != null) {\n            classicGroup.add(\n                new ClassicGroupMember(\n                    joiningMember.memberId(),\n                    Optional.ofNullable(joiningMember.instanceId()),\n                    joiningMember.clientId(),\n                    joiningMember.clientHost(),\n                    joiningMember.rebalanceTimeoutMs(),\n                    joiningMember.classicProtocolSessionTimeout().get(),\n                    ConsumerProtocol.PROTOCOL_TYPE,\n                    joiningMember.supportedJoinGroupRequestProtocols(),\n                    null\n                )\n            );\n        }\n\n        classicGroup.setProtocolName(Optional.of(classicGroup.selectProtocol()));\n        classicGroup.setSubscribedTopics(classicGroup.computeSubscribedTopics());\n\n        classicGroup.allMembers().forEach(classicGroupMember -> {\n            // Set the assignment with serializing the ConsumerGroup's targetAssignment.\n            // The serializing version should align with that of the member's JoinGroupRequestProtocol.\n            String memberId = classicGroupMember.memberId();\n            if (joiningMember != null && memberId.equals(joiningMember.memberId())) {\n                // If the downgraded is triggered by the joining static member replacing\n                // the leaving static member, the joining member should take the assignment\n                // of the leaving one.\n                ConsumerGroupMember replacedMember = consumerGroup.staticMember(joiningMember.instanceId());\n                if (replacedMember == null) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"joiningMember must be a static member when not null.\");\n                }\n                memberId = replacedMember.memberId();\n            }\n            byte[] assignment = Utils.toArray(ConsumerProtocol.serializeAssignment(\n                toConsumerProtocolAssignment(\n                    consumerGroup.targetAssignment().get(memberId).partitions(),\n                    image\n                ),\n                ConsumerProtocol.deserializeVersion(\n                    ByteBuffer.wrap(classicGroupMember.metadata(classicGroup.protocolName().orElse(\"\")))\n                )\n            ));\n\n            classicGroupMember.setAssignment(assignment);\n        });\n\n        return classicGroup;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Populate the record list with the records needed to create the given classic group.\n     *\n     * @param records           The list to which the new records are added.\n     */\n    public void createClassicGroupRecords(\n        List<CoordinatorRecord> records\n    ) {\n        Map<String, byte[]> assignments = new HashMap<>();\n        allMembers().forEach(classicGroupMember ->\n            assignments.put(classicGroupMember.memberId(), classicGroupMember.assignment())\n        );\n\n        records.add(GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newGroupMetadataRecord(this, assignments));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Checks whether the transition to the target state is valid.\n     *\n     * @param targetState the target state to transition to.\n     */\n    private void assertValidTransition(ClassicGroupState targetState) {\n        if (!targetState.validPreviousStates().contains(state)) {\n Remove all dynamic members that have not rejoined\n     * during this stage and proceed with the next generation for this group. The generation id\n     * is incremented and the group transitions to CompletingRebalance state if there is at least\n     * one member.\n     *\n     * If the group is in Empty state, append a new group metadata record to the log. Otherwise,\n     * complete all members' join group response futures and wait for sync requests from members.\n     *\n     * @param group The group that is completing the join group phase.\n     *\n     * @return The coordinator result that will be appended to the log.\n     */\n    private CoordinatorResult<Void, CoordinatorRecord> completeClassicGroupJoin(\n        ClassicGroup group\n    ) {\n        timer.cancel(classicGroupJoinKey(group.groupId()));\n        String groupId = group.groupId();\n\n        Map<String, ClassicGroupMember> notYetRejoinedDynamicMembers =\n            group.notYetRejoinedMembers().entrySet().stream()\n                .filter(entry -> !entry.getValue().isStaticMember())\n                .collect(Collectors.toMap(Map.Entry::getKey, Map.Entry::getValue));\n\n        if (!notYetRejoinedDynamicMembers.isEmpty()) {\n            notYetRejoinedDynamicMembers.values().forEach(failedMember -> {\n                group.remove(failedMember.memberId());\n                timer.cancel(classicGroupHeartbeatKey(group.groupId(), failedMember.memberId()));\n            });\n\n            log.info(\"Group {} removed dynamic members who haven't joined: {}\",\n                groupId, notYetRejoinedDynamicMembers.keySet());\n        }\n\n        if (group.isInState(DEAD)) {\n            log.info(\"Group {} is dead, skipping rebalance stage.\", groupId);\n        } else if (!group.maybeElectNewJoinedLeader() && !group.allMembers().isEmpty()) {\n            // If all members are not rejoining, we will postpone the completion\n            // of rebalance preparing stage, and send out another delayed operation\n            // until session timeout removes all the non-responsive members.\n            log.error(\"Group {} could not complete rebalance because no members rejoined.\", groupId);\n\n            timer.schedule(\n                classicGroupJoinKey(groupId),\n                group.rebalanceTimeoutMs(),\n                TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS,\n                false,\n                () -> completeClassicGroupJoin(group.groupId())\n            );\n\n            return EMPTY_RESULT;\n        } else {\n            group.initNextGeneration();\n            if (group.isInState(EMPTY)) {\n                log.info(\"Group {} with generation {} is now empty.\", groupId, group.generationId());\n\n                CompletableFuture<Void> appendFuture = new CompletableFuture<>();\n                appendFuture.whenComplete((__, t) -> {\n                    if (t != null) {\n                        // We failed to write the empty group metadata. Each represents a distinct code path that can be reached in production.\n\n---\n\n## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests\n\n### Failure Mode 1: SyncGroup Append Failure Leaves Consumer-Group Member Stuck Forever\n\n- **Risk**: HIGH\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 7601\n  (`classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup`)\n- **Description**: When a member using the classic wire protocol sends a `SyncGroup`\n  request to a group that has already been upgraded to the modern consumer-group type,\n  the handler at `classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup` (line 7584) creates an\n  `appendFuture` and calls `appendFuture.whenComplete(...)`. The callback **only\n  handles the success branch** (`if (t == null) { ... }`). There is no `else` clause\n  and no error path. If the log write fails (e.g., the broker loses partition\n  leadership mid-write), `responseFuture` is **never completed**, and the caller\n  blocks indefinitely.\n\n  The analogous path for a pure classic group, `classicGroupSyncToClassicGroup`\n  (line 7486), correctly handles failure at lines 7538\u20137542\n  (`resetAndPropagateAssignmentWithError` + `maybePrepareRebalanceOrCompleteJoin`).\n  The consumer-group path has no equivalent guard, making the failure asymmetric and\n  invisible in tests. `testSyncGroupAsLeaderAppendFailureTransformsError` (line 8878)\n  covers the classic path only.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testClassicGroupSyncToConsumerGroupAppendFailureCompletesResponseFuture()\n      throws Exception {\n      String groupId = Would also validate that the\n  `responseFuture` is always completed (success or error) regardless of log-write\n  outcome.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Sync-Phase Expiry Timer Fires With Stale Generation ID\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 7241\n  (`expirePendingSync`)\n- **Description**: When the coordinator transitions a classic group through a\n  rebalance it schedules a sync-expiry timer keyed on the current `generationId`.\n  If the group rebalances again before that timer fires (incrementing the generation\n  to `N+1`), the timer callback eventually calls `expirePendingSync(groupId, N)`.\n\n  At line 7253\u20137255 the code checks `if (generationId != group.generationId())` and\n  **only emits an error log**, then returns `EMPTY_RESULT`. The members that are\n  awaiting sync in generation `N+1` are not cleaned up by this call. The sync-expiry\n  timer for generation `N+1` was scheduled with a separate key derived from the new\n  generation, so no orphaned member cleanup happens from the stale timer. In the\n  normal operating path this is benign, but if the new-generation timer was cancelled\n  or missed (e.g., due to a bug in `removeSyncExpiration`), members hang with no\n  further timeout.\n\n  No existing test triggers the mismatch branch; all tests either use a single\n  generation or advance time by exactly the right amount.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testExpirePendingSyncWithStaleGenerationIdIsNoOp() throws Exception {\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext context = new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.Builder()\n          .build();\n      int rebalanceTimeoutMs = 5_000;\n      int sessionTimeoutMs   = 30_000;\n\n      // Join three members so we get generation 1.\n      List<JoinGroupResponseData> gen1Responses =\n          context.joinWithNMembers(\"group-id\", 3, rebalanceTimeoutMs, sessionTimeoutMs);\n      ClassicGroup group =\n          context.groupMetadataManager.getOrMaybeCreateClassicGroup(\"group-id\", false);\n      assertEquals(1, group.generationId());\n\n      // Leader sends sync \u2192 group transitions to STABLE.\n      GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncResult syncResult = context.sendClassicGroupSync(\n          new GroupMetadataManagerTestContext.SyncGroupRequestBuilder()\n              .withGroupId(\"group-id\")\n              .withMemberId(gen1Responses.get(0).memberId())\n              .withGenerationId(1)\n              .build());\n      syncResult.appendFuture.complete(null);\n      assertTrue(group.isInState(STABLE));\n\n      // Trigger a second rebalance \u2192 generation 2.\n      gen1Responses.get(0).setMemberId(gen1Responses.get(0).memberId()); Also\n  validates the contract that stale timer callbacks produce no observable side-effects\n  on the current group generation.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Follower Leaves Group During COMPLETING_REBALANCE \u2014 Sync Future Hangs\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 8098\n  (`removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`); `ClassicGroup.java` ~line 478 (`remove`)\n- **Description**: After the join phase completes and the group enters\n  `COMPLETING_REBALANCE`, each follower that calls `SyncGroup` has its\n  `CompletableFuture<SyncGroupResponseData>` stored in\n  `ClassicGroupMember.awaitingSyncFuture` (set at line 7503). If the follower\n  subsequently sends a `LeaveGroup` request, `removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`\n  (line 8098\u20138118) is called. That method:\n\n  1. Cancels the heartbeat timer.\n  2. Calls `group.completeJoinFuture(member, ...)` \u2014 completes the *join* future.\n  3. Calls `group.remove(member.memberId())`.\n\n  `ClassicGroup.remove` (line 478\u2013496) removes the member from the members map and\n  pending-sync list, but **does not complete `awaitingSyncFuture`**. The\n  `CompletableFuture` returned to the follower's `SyncGroup` handler is permanently\n  stuck pending. The network connection holds a reference to it and will never\n  deliver a response to the client, leaking a future and leaving the consumer in a\n  blocked state.\n\n  No existing test sends a `LeaveGroup` from a follower that has already submitted\n  its sync request (i.e., after `setAwaitingSyncFuture` has been called).\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void **Coverage Delta**: Exercises the code path where `group.remove()` is called for a\n  member that has an outstanding `awaitingSyncFuture`. Currently the\n  `awaitingSyncFuture` field is never checked inside `remove()` or\n  `removeCurrentMemberFromClassicGroup`, so the test would expose the missing\n  completion and drive a fix. Covers lines 8098\u20138118 in `GroupMetadataManager` and\n  lines 478\u2013496 in `ClassicGroup` in the `COMPLETING_REBALANCE` scenario.\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Static Consumer-Group Member Temporary Leave Silently Discards Pending Revocations\n\n- **Risk**: MEDIUM\n- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 4137\n  (`consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave`)\n- **Description**: When a static member sends a heartbeat with\n  `memberEpoch == LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH (-2)`, the coordinator calls\n  `consumerGroupStaticMemberGroupLeave`. At line 4142\u20134145 a new member record is\n  built that sets `partitionsPendingRevocation` to **an empty map**:\n\n  ```java\n  ConsumerGroupMember leavingStaticMember = new ConsumerGroupMember.Builder(member)\n      .setMemberEpoch(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH)\n      .setPartitionsPendingRevocation(Map.of())   // silently clears!\n      .build();\n  ```\n\n  If the member was in `UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS` state (i.e., it had partitions it had\n  not yet revoked), those partitions are erased from the coordinator's record without\n  triggering any reassignment. When the member rejoins before the session timeout\n  (using `memberEpoch == 0`), the coordinator re-assigns it partitions from scratch.\n  Another member that was waiting for those partitions to be freed may now hold them\n  concurrently, violating partition exclusivity.\n\n  The existing test `testNoGroupEpochBumpWhenStaticMemberTemporarilyLeaves` (line\n  2518) only uses a member whose state .setMemberEpoch(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH));\n\n      // Verify the response carries LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH.\n      assertEquals(LEAVE_GROUP_STATIC_MEMBER_EPOCH, There is therefore\n  a temporal window between the call to `onTopicsDeleted` (which adds tombstones to\n  the output batch) and their replay. If `replayEndTransactionMarker` is processed\n  for a COMMIT in that window, it will find the pending transactional offsets for\n  the deleted topic still present in `pendingTransactionalOffsets` and **commit\n  them** to the main `offsets` store. Those committed offsets then survive, even\n  though the topic was deleted and tombstones were queued. The subsequent tombstone\n  replay removes the committed offsets, but a compacted log may not contain the\n  tombstone, leaving a residual committed offset for a non-existent topic after a\n  broker restart.\n\n  All four existing `testOnTopicsDeleted*` tests (lines 3541, 3586, 3611, 3632)\n  operate only on committed offsets; none inject transactional offsets before\n  calling `deleteTopics`.\n\n- **Proposed Test**:\n  ```java\n  @Test\n  public void testOnTopicsDeletedPurgesPendingTransactionalOffsets() {\n      OffsetMetadataManagerTestContext context =\n          new tombstones.\n      assertEquals(2, records.size(),\n          \"Both committed and pending transactional offsets must be tombstoned\");\n\n      // Replay the tombstones (simulates the runtime writing The members that are\n  awaiting sync in generation `N+1` are not cleaned up by this call. The sync-expiry\n  timer for generation `N+1` was scheduled with a separate key derived from the new\n  generation, so no orphaned member cleanup happens from the stale timer. In the\n  normal operating path this is benign, but if the new-generation timer was cancelled\n  or missed (e.g., due to a bug in `removeSyncExpiration`), members hang with no\n  further timeout.\n\n  No existing test triggers the mismatch branch; # Test Coverage Gap Analysis: Kafka Consumer Group Coordinator

## Summary

The Kafka consumer group coordinator has undergone a major Java rewrite. The primary
implementation now lives in:

- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java`
  (~8,800 lines) — core group lifecycle, join/sync/heartbeat/leave logic for classic
  and modern consumer groups.
- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java`
  — offset commit, fetch, expiry, transactional offset handling.
- `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java`
  — state machine and member tracking for classic (pre-KIP-848) groups.

Tests live in:
- `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManagerTest.java`
  (~25,900 lines, 377 `@Test` methods)
- `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManagerTest.java`
- `group-coordinator/src/test/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorServiceTest.java`

Despite broad coverage, five concrete failure modes are not exercised by any existing
test. Each represents a distinct code path that can be reached in production.

---

## Failure Modes and Proposed Tests

### Failure Mode 1: SyncGroup Append Failure Leaves Consumer-Group Member Stuck Forever

- **Risk**: HIGH
- **Code Location**: `GroupMetadataManager.java` ~line 7601
  (`classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup`)
- **Description**: When a member using the classic wire protocol sends a `SyncGroup`
  request to a group that has already been upgraded to the modern consumer-group type,
  the handler at `classicGroupSyncToConsumerGroup` (line 7584) creates an
  `appendFuture` and calls `appendFuture.when
... (truncated)
